AOW_btn_export_data = {
	potential = { from = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_hide_main_interface } } }
	allow = { #别在同一天导出数据了，不好处理
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "AOW_requires_do_not_export_data_on_the_same_day"
			NOT = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_is_exporting_data }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_export_data_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			AOW_eft_GLBL_export_data = yes
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_is_exporting_data days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_default_1_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			AOW_eft_GLBL_default_balance_variable = { TYPE = set }
		}
	}
}

				inline_script = AOW_btn_preinstall_custom/game
			}
		}
	}
}

#零者
AOW_btn_preinstall_laquly = {
	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_laquly_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }

	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_ZaiXiaKuangFeng_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 100 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 100 }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 10 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 10 KEY = space_arena }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 3 VA = 1 KEY = space_sensor_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 10 KEY = habitat }

#Ayame
AOW_btn_preinstall_Ayame = {
	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_default_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				#平衡数值
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = -10 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 10 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 5 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = -1000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = -1000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 50 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 2000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 500 }
				#巨构上限
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 10 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = space_arena }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = space_sensor_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = habitat }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = hyper_relay }

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 1 KEY = mega_art_installation }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = mega_shipyard }

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 1 KEY = deep_space_prison }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = nanites_activator }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = nanites_transmutation }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = naval_command_base }

	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_Huifon_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = -1000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = -1000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 2000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 2000 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 500 }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = space_arena }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = space_sensor_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = habitat }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = hyper_relay }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = orbital_ring }

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = satellite_defense_base }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = interstellar_assembly }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = mega_art_installation }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = mega_shipyard }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = quantum_catapult }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = spy_orb }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = strategic_coordination_center }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = think_tank }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 0 VA = 0 KEY = hyperlane_controller }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 0 VA = 0 KEY = advanced_hyperlane_controller }

#atk专属
AOW_btn_preinstall_atk = {
	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_atk_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 5 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 5 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 10 }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 5 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 5 KEY = space_arena }

#龙神longshen
AOW_btn_preinstall_LongShen = {
	potential = { from = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_page_presets } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_default_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				#平衡数值
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 0 }
				#巨构上限
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = space_arena }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = 1 VA = 0 KEY = space_sensor_station }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = habitat }

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = nanites_activator }
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = nanites_transmutation }
